    Yang Zang Decoction: Treats frequent white diarrhea.

    Ingredients:
    1 tael of prepared Dang Gui (Angelica)
    1 tael of dried Wu Mei (black plum) meat
    1 tael of dried ginger
    1 tael of Huang Qi (Astragalus)
    1 tael of boiled Bai Zhu (Atractylodes)
    1 tael of dragon bones

    Crush and grind them into a fine powder. Take 1 qian (a small measure) with a small cup of water, add a little fresh ginger and millet, decoct until reduced by half, strain, and take warm before milk meals, adjusting dosage as necessary.

    Xiang Lian Pill: Treats both red and white diarrhea, thirst, and pain.

    Ingredients:
    1 tael of prepared Huang Lian (Coptis), finely chopped, stir-fried with Wu Zhu Yu (Evodia) until fragrant, then remove the Wu Zhu Yu;
    2.5 qian of dried Wu Mei meat, thinly sliced and slowly roasted on a new tile;
    0.5 tael of Nan Mu Xiang (Cardamom); do not overheat.

    Grind these into powder. Use 0.5 tael of prepared E Jiao (Colla Corii Asini), finely chopped, stir-fry until puffed, then hydrate with water to form a paste. Once cooled, combine with the previous powder, mix thoroughly in a mortar, and form into pills the size of hemp seeds. For red diarrhea, take 33 to 55 pills, or 77 pills, with an empty stomach and drink with licorice decoction. For white diarrhea, use the same number of pills with white ginger decoction; for mixed symptoms, take with warm clear rice soup on an empty stomach.

    Jin Su Pill: Treats red and white diarrhea and undigested food in the stomach.

    Ingredients:
    1 tael of prepared Huang Lian
    0.5 tael of Chuan Xiong (Szechuan lovage)
    0.5 tael of Zhi Guo (the fruit of the bitter orange)
    0.5 tael of germinated barley, washed and roasted
    0.5 tael of red Fu Ling (Hoelen)
    0.5 tael of Bai Zhi (Angelica dahurica)
    0.5 tael of Mu Xiang (Costus root)

    Grind all except the Mu Xiang, which should not be overheated; roast the other six ingredients and combine them with the Mu Xiang into powder. Use 1 tael of Shen Qu (fermented barley) to make a paste, and form into pills the size of millet. Take 70 to 100 pills on an empty stomach with warm clear rice drink, at any time.[43p]

    Zhi Fu Wan from Wang's Hand Collection - Treats children's pure pus dysentery, effective like magic. One piece of large Fuzi.

    First, use pig fat to extract about half a cup of oil, then coat the Fuzi to crack it. Remove and let it cool, peel off the skin and navel, grind it into a fine powder, and mix it with date flesh to form pills the size of mung beans. Take five to seven pills at a time, up to fifteen or twenty, and swallow with rice wine on an empty stomach before meals.

    Zhu Family Heritage Recipe - Treats children's white pus cold dysentery with cramping pain below the navel. Equal parts of Hawthorn skin and Qingmuxiang.

    Grind into a powder, mix with polished rice to form pills the size of mung beans, and take five pills with rice wine.

    Fuzi San - Transmitted by Changsha physician Ding Shifa for children's malnutrition dysentery, often with white pus and abdominal pain. One piece of Fuzi (peeled and prepared), half a tael of Longgu and Chishizhi, one fen each of Mitaoseng, Huangdan, Hu Fen (fried), and burned cuttlefish bone, and one fen of Chishaoyao.

    Grind these into a powder, taking half a qian each time with rice wine, three times a day.

    Blood Dysentery Formula - Treats children's heat toxins.

    Ten fen of Xijiao, six fen of Dihu, three fen of honey, and five he of Dimaicao. Chop the four ingredients, boil with three sheng of water until two sheng remain, strain, and dose according to the child's size.[45p]

    　　马齿菜汁粥 【《圣惠》】 　治小儿血痢不瘥。　　马齿菜汁一合　蜜半合　粟米一合[46p]

    Preparation of Medicinal Formulas for Treating Child's Bloody Dysentery

    Ingredients:

    • Three taels of scallion whites
    • Three volumes of fragrant soybeans
    • Seven pieces of gardenia fruit
    • One tael of coptis

    Instructions:

    1. Cut the four ingredients mentioned above.
    2. Use three sheng of water to boil them down to nine dou.
    3. Strain the mixture and divide it for consumption.

    Additional Recipe from "Waí Tái" by Liu:
    For treating child's bloody dysentery:

    • Six fen each of earth poppy, wine yellow bark, and river coptis
    • Two fen of horse mint
    • One tael of madder root
    • Three fen of fresh ginger

    Instructions:

    1. Cut the seven ingredients.
    2. Use two sheng of water to boil them down to one sheng.
    3. Divide the mixture according to the child’s size, with a dosage ranging from one dou to two dou.

    Another Recipe from "Shi Yi Xin Jian":
    For treating child's bloody dysentery:

    • One dou of fresh purslane juice

    Instructions:

    1. Mix the juice with one spoonful of honey and take on an empty stomach.

    Coptis Powder from "Sheng Hui":
    For treating child's bloody dysentery with fever and dry mouth and abdominal pain:

    • One tael of coptis (lightly roasted without hairs)
    • One tael each of rhinoceros horn powder, white sacred lotus root, and yellow scutellaria
    • One tael each of creeping root and woad
    • Three fen of white-headed翁 (plant)
    • Half a tael each of roasted licorice and sliced angelica (lightly roasted)

    Instructions:

    1. Grind the above ingredients into a coarse powder.
    2. For each dose, take one qian, dissolve it in one small cup of water, boil it down to five fen, strain, and adjust the dosage according to the child's size.

    For treating child's bloody dysentery that does not heal:

    Water Plantain treats blood dysentery and deficiency.

    Burned and powdered snake skin and chicken豆 shell, each one tael; half a tael of Coptis and water plantain, all ground into fine powder. Then use half a tael of vermilion, true aloe, cattle bile, and powdered frost, finely ground. Mix all these ingredients well and grind them finely again. Take five to seven pills the size of millet rice with a musk decoction, adjusting according to the child's size.

    Madder root decoction treats unresolved blood dysentery.

    Grated madder root, grated earth chestnut, Coptis without the beard, calcined red stone resin, and cooked donkey-hide gelatin, all one tael; half a tael of roasted licorice and yellow root. Grind all these herbs into fine powder, and take one penny weight mixed with eight parts water, boil down to five parts, strain, and drink warm.

    Thick Intestine pill treats blood dysentery with intestinal weakness.

    Coptis and Fructus Meliae, each one tael; half a tael each of Aromatic Wood, cooked donkey-hide gelatin with clam powder stir-fried, lightly fried Evodia, and when washed and baked, Angelica sinensis. Grind all these into fine powder, mix with rice and form into pills the size of millet rice, take ten pills with rice drink before dairy meals, adjusting according to the child's size.

    Saintly Efficacy Powder treats prolonged blood dysentery.

    Calcined red stone resin, calcined white dragon bone, and cooked donkey-hide gelatin, each one tael; half a tael each of Bael fruit peel, Aromatic Wood, roasted ginger, Coptis, and roasted licorice. Grind all these into fine powder, take half a penny weight, boiled with millet drink and take before meals.[47p]

    　　必效丹　治血痢烦并。
    　　川黄连去须，二两　大枣半升　干姜一两　白矾半两　　右件用瓦器盛，盐泥固济，留一窍子，以木炭火烧，烟息为度，取出捣罗为末，白面糊和丸黍米大，每服十粒，米饮下，量儿大小加减。　　又方　治小儿热痢下血。

    Must-Efficacious Elixir for treating blood dysentery with irritability.

    Remove the husk from two taels of Sichuan Huanglian, half a liter of large dates, one tael of dried ginger, and half a tael of white alum. Place the above ingredients in a clay vessel, seal with salt mud, leaving a small opening, and heat with charcoal until the smoke ceases. Take it out, grind and sift into a fine powder, and mix it with wheat flour to form pills the size of millet. Take ten pills each time, swallowed with rice drink, adjusting the dosage based on the child's size.

    Another Recipe for treating children's heat dysentery with blood.

    Take half a tael of Huangbo without skin and four qian of red peony. Grind them into fine powder and mix with rice to form pills the size of sesame seeds. Take one to twenty pills before meals with rice drink, increasing the number for larger children.

    Another Recipe passed down in the Ji family for treating children's dysentery with blood.

    Grind Xuanlian into powder. Use chicken egg to mold it into a cake, heat it over charcoal until red, then cover it to avoid loss of gas. Once cooled, finely grind this and take half a qian with rice drink, adjusting the dosage as needed.

    Another Recipe using half a qian of fine turmeric powder. Mix with hot water and administer.

    Ji's Dihu Powder for treating children’s blood dysentery that has endured for a long time.

    One part Dihu, stir-fried, five roasted Heshou, skin removed, and one qian each of stir-fried Chen Huan and Huanglian, all stir-fried. Grind into fine powder and take half a qian or one qian with aged rice drink.[48p]

    Bai Tou Weng Pill
    Three parts of Bai Tou Weng, six parts of Huang Lian, grind three parts of pomegranate peel. Combine these three ingredients with three sheng of water, boil down to eight hé. For children under forty days, take five hé divided into three doses. For larger children, increase the dosage. In another recipe, omit the pomegranate peel and use three parts of rhinoceros horn shavings.

    Zhou Hou Nursing Mother's Recipe
    One sheng of roasted and dried broad bean stems, three taels of ginseng.
    Combine these with three sheng of water, decoct to one sheng and a half, strain out the dregs to obtain the juice, and cook millet porridge to feed the nursing mother; it’s effective.

    Zhou Hou's Near-Efficacious Recipe
    For treating a three-year-old child suffering from dysentery, initially with more blood than pus, then after four days with more pus than blood, with over forty occurrences day and night.
    Five small hé of raw Rehmannia juice, one small hé of sheep kidney fat.
    Warm the kidney fat first, and divide into three or four doses, showing immediate effect. The nursing mother must refrain from taking it, and there’s also a recipe for the nursing mother above.

    Sheng Hui Wu Lan Powder
    For treating children's dysentery with pus and blood like fish brains, and abdominal pain.
    One tael each of Wu Lan, Chuan Sheng Ma, Chi Shao Yao, and calcined dragon bone; half a tael of Zhi Zi Ren.
    Grind these herbs coarsely and sift to make a powder. For each dose, take one qian, mix with one cup of water, add three or seven grains of fermented soybeans, boil down to five parts, strain out the dregs, and without regard for the time, adjust the dosage according to the size of the child and warm for consumption.[49p]

    　　樗根皮散　治小儿脓血痢如鱼脑，困重。　　臭樗根皮一分，銼炒微黄　枳壳去瓤微炒　黄连去须微炒　芜荑微炒　赤芍药各半两　　右件药捣粗罗为散，每服一钱，以水一小盏，入豉三十粒，葱白一茎，煎至六分，去滓，不计时候，量儿大小分减温服。
    　　人参散　治小儿脓血痢，多时不瘥，腹痛羸瘦，不欲饮食。　　人参　当归微炒　地榆　阿胶捣碎炒令黄燥　黄连　子芩　黄蘗炙　赤芍　白芜荑微炒　厚朴去粗皮，生姜汁炙令香熟，各半两　　右件药捣粗罗为散，每服一钱，以水一小盏，入薤白一茎，豉五十粒，煎至五分，去滓，不计时候，量儿大小分减温服。

    Chuan Gen Pi San: Treats children's purulent blood dysentery resembling fish brain, causing heaviness.

    Ingredients:

    • Stinky chuan root bark (1 part), roasted until slightly yellow
    • Bitter orange peel (deseeded, slightly roasted)
    • Coptis chinensis (root, slightly roasted)
    • Wormwood (slightly roasted)
    • Red peony root (½ tael each of the first 4 ingredients)

    Directions: Grind the above ingredients coarsely, sift to create a powder. For each dose, take 1 qian (one-tenth of a tael), mix with a small cup of water, add 30 grains of fermented soybeans, and one stalk of scallion. Boil until reduced to 60%. Strain, and depending on the child's size, adjust and give warm.

    Ren Shen San: Treats children's purulent blood dysentery, prolonged sickness, abdominal pain, emaciation, and loss of appetite.

    Ingredients:

    • Ginseng
    • Angelica sinensis (slightly roasted)
    • Ground knotgrass
    • Ejiao (crushed and roasted until yellow)
    • Coptis chinensis (deseeded)
    • Scutellaria (honey roasted)
    • Rhizoma coptidis (shallow-roasted)
    • Red peony root
    • White wormwood (slightly roasted)
    • Magnolia bark (outer skin removed), soaked in ginger juice and roasted until fragrant (½ tael each of the first 9 ingredients)

    Directions: Grind the above ingredients coarsely, sift to create a powder. For each dose, take 1 qian, mix with a small cup of water, add one stalk of garlic and 50 grains of fermented soybeans. Boil until reduced to 50%. Strain, and depending on the child's size, adjust and give warm.

    Ji Shi Fan Wan: Treats children's purulent blood dysentery that does not heal, gradually leading to weakness.

    Ingredients:

    • Chicken feces alum ash
    • Dragon bone
    • Ejiao (crushed and roasted until yellow)
    • Coptis chinensis (deseeded, slightly roasted) (1 tael each)
    • Hu powder (1 part, roasted until slightly yellow)

    Directions: Grind the above ingredients to a fine powder, mix with concentrated vinegar to form a paste, then roll into pills the size of mung beans. For each dosage, take seven pills with warm water, three to four times a day, adjusting according to the child's size.[50p]

    　　黄连阿胶丸　治小儿热痢下重，脓血疼痛，腹中痛不可忍。　　真川黄连去须，一两半　白茯苓　白芍药炒　阿胶杵碎，慢火炒如珠子白色，别杵为细末，各半两　　右上三味为细末，斟酌米酢多少，熬胶得所，和匀入臼杵万下，众手丸如菉豆大，每服自二十丸为始，至于五十丸，食前温米饮下，日二三，以知为度。未知，加药更丸一等如黄米大，与小儿服。

    Huanglian Ejiao Wan treats children's severe heat dysentery with pus and blood, causing unbearable abdominal pain.

    True Sichuan Huanglian without hair, one and a half taels; Bai Fuling, Bai Shao Yao, stir-fried; Ejiao, crushed, slowly stir-fried until pearl-white; separate and grind into fine powder, each half a tael.

    Combine the three powdered ingredients, adjust the amount of rice vinegar to obtain the right consistency, blend well in a mortar and pestle, shape into pills the size of mung beans. Take starting with twenty pills up to fifty, with warm rice drink before meals, two to three times a day, adjusting as needed. If unknown, add more medicine in pills the size of yellow millet for the child to take.

    Fanfa San treats intestinal inflammation with pus and blood.

    Bai Shizhi, one fen, grayness; Licorice, roasted, each two fen. Grind these into powder, mix with rice juice to form a paste, take twice daily.

    Zhang Huan Jianwei Dan treats dysentery with pus and blood, resulting in gradual weight loss.

    Huanglian, one tael, washed and lightly roasted; Ku Bai Fan, one fen; Wu Mei flesh, roasted; Longgu, Bai Shizhi, Shenqu, roasted; Gan Jiang, each half a tael.

    Crush and sift these into fine powder, mix with vinegar to create a dough, shape into pills the size of millet. Take ten pills with rice drink, adjusting dosage according to the child's size.[51p]

    小儿痢门

    　　　　方

    　　通神丸 【《证治准绳》，下同】 　治小儿大人，痢下脓血，里急腰重，脐腹疼痛。　　没药　净五露脂　乳香各一钱，俱细研炒　巴豆七枚，去心膜，压出油　　右四味同研令细匀，滴水为丸如粟米大，每服一粒，生木瓜研水下，不拘时候。
    　　鲊汤丸　治小儿泻痢五色脓血，如烂鱼肠，并无大便，只是脓血，肠中搅痛。　　粉霜　轻粉　硇砂各一钱　朱砂抄一钱匕　白丁香四钱　乳香半钱，别研　巴豆七粒，去油　　右为末，蒸枣肉丸，每服婴孩三丸如粟米大，二三岁如大麻子大，四五岁亦如麻子大，并旋(上绝下刀)成丸，煎鲊鱼汤吞下，一日二服，间调胃气药与之。[52p]

    Qing Ju Dan

    To treat the intersection of hot and cold, mixed red and white pus and blood.
    Soak Qing Ju Pi in broth to remove the white and roast it; wash and roast Dang Gui with wine; take one tael each of Huang Lian and Gan Jiang; half a tael each of Hou Po, Sheng Jiang, and Rou Dou Kou.
    Pound and sieve the above ingredients into a fine powder, mix with white flour to form pills the size of millet. Take ten pills with rice wine before meals.

    Children's Dysentery

    Formula: Tong Shen Wan
    To treat dysentery with pus and blood in children and adults, with urgency in the bowels, heavy waist, and abdominal pain.
    Take Mo Yao, Qing Lu Zhi, and Ru Xiang, each one qian, finely ground and roasted; seven pieces of Ba Dou, remove the heart and membrane, press to extract oil.
    Grind all four ingredients finely and evenly, add water to form pills the size of millet. Take one pill with the juice of raw papaya, without time restriction.

    Zha Tang Wan
    To treat children's diarrhea and dysentery with five colors of pus and blood, as if it were rotten fish intestines, with no proper stools, only pus and blood, accompanied by intestinal cramps.
    Take Fen Shuang, Qing Fen, and Nao Sha, each one qian; one qian of Zhu Sha by the spoon; four qian of Bai Ding Xiang; half a qian of Ru Xiang, ground separately.
    Use seven pieces of Ba Dou, remove the oil.
    Grind into powder, steam with jujube meat to form pills. For infants, take three pills the size of millet; for two or three-year-olds, the size of large hemp seeds; for four or five-year-olds, also the size of hemp seeds; form into pills by rolling them. Take with broth from Zha fish, twice a day, interspersed with stomach-regulating medicine.[52p]

    　　地榆饮　治三十六种内下五色恶物，心神烦热不止。　　地榆　白茯苓　黄蘗炙，各一两
    　　右为末，每服一钱，水一盏，煎至五分，去滓，分三服。
    　　三霜丸　治小儿赤白或五色杂痢。
    　　巴豆去皮，拣白色肥好者三钱研细，先用白绵绢包三二十重，次用纸包压令油尽，取二钱，轻者为用　真轻粉　粉霜各二钱　　右三味，同研匀极细，别取好黄蜡三钱，酒煮三二十沸，取出，去酒令净，再熔入药和之。如无煮酒，蜡亦堪用。和成剂，油单内盛。如服食，旋丸如小菉豆大，三岁以下如粟米大，每服二三丸，温熟水下，量儿大小加减。[53p]

    Diyu Drink treats thirty-six types of internal evils in five colors, alleviating persistent heat and agitation of the spirit.
    Diyu, white poria, and yellow bristle are each one tael.
    Grind these to a powder; for each dose, take one qian, mix with one cup of water, and boil until reduced by half. Strain out the residue and divide into three doses.

    San Shuang Pills treat children's red-white or mixed diarrhea in five colors.
    Remove the skin from three qian of good quality white banana seeds and grind them finely. First, wrap in fine white silk cloth in several layers, then wrap in paper and press until the oil is exhausted. Take two qian of this, along with two qian each of light powder and powdered frost, mix all three ingredients into an extremely fine powder. Separately prepare three qian of good yellow wax, boil with wine until bubbling, remove, let the wine evaporate, and then melt the wax back into the medicine. If there is no boiled wine, wax can still be used. Form into pills, keeping them inside an oil paper. For dosage, make pills the size of small beans, and for children under three years old, the size of millet. Take two to three pills with warm water, adjusting the amount based on the child's size.[53p]

    　　吉氏家传方　治五色痢兼渴不止。
    　　茯苓　宣黄连　黄蘗各等分
    　　右件取黄蘗末，以浆水和面糊，良久和前二味为丸如菉豆大，三岁米饮下七丸。杀疳，熟水下五丸。
    　　至圣丸
    　　厚朴姜制　黄蘗以鸡子白炙黄熟，干再上　当归酒浸　　右三味等分细末，炼蜜为丸如梧桐子大，小儿细丸，厚朴汤下，每服四十丸加减。
    　　定粉散　治疳痢五色痢。

    Jishi Family Prescription for Treating Five-Colored Dysentery with Constant Thirst

    Ingredients:

    • Poria
    • Huang Lian (Coptis)
    • Huang Bo (Phellodendron) - equal parts of each

    Instructions:
    Take the powdered Huang Bo, mix it with water to form a paste. After a while, combine it with the previous two ingredients to form pills about the size of mung beans. For children of three years old, take seven pills with a rice drink. For killing dysentery, take five pills with boiled water.

    Zhisheng Pills:

    • Thick Magnolia Bark (Hou Pu)
    • Ginger
    • Huang Bo, roasted with egg white until a deep yellow, dried and roasted again
    • Dang Gui (Angelica) soaked in wine

    Combine these three ingredients into fine powder, then make pills with honey, shaped like the size of a firm seed. For children, make smaller pills. Take with Hou Pu decoction; each dose is forty pills, adjusted as needed.

    Dingfen Powder:
    Treats dysentery and five-colored dysentery.

    • Dingfen
    • Dragon Bone
    • Yellow Lead, calcined, each two qian (a unit of weight)
    • Three pieces of Heshou (Chebula), cooked thoroughly

    Grind the above into powder. For each dose, take half a qian mixed with gruel drink. For those over three years, use half a qian.

    Fermented Milk Method:
    Treats children's tight mouth dysentery.

    • Thick Magnolia Bark
    • Zhi Ke (bitter orange), five fen each
    • Bai Zhu (Atractylodes)
    • Shao Yao (Paeonia) half a liang each
    • Talc, one liang
    • Mu Tong (Akebia)
    • Chen Pi (aged tangerine peel)
    • Gan Cao (licorice), five fen each

    Grind these into four separate fine powders, plus seven peach kernels. Mix with two and a half cups of water, take one cup for the mother to drink. During the dose, eliminate any remaining milk for best results.[54p]

    Resting Dysentery Prescription

    From "Zhou Hou," for treating persistent dysentery.

    Dragon bone, roasted until yellow and charred, pounded and taken in a dose the size of a thumb, three times a day will bring recovery.

    Another Prescription:
    Four ounces of dragon bone, pounded to the size of small beans, boiled in five liters of water until reduced to two and a half liters, cooled, and divided into five doses, will be effective.

    Preserving Life Trustworthy Efficacious Muffins: For treating all forms of lumps, accumulations, stagnation, and other conditions persisting for ten to twenty years.

    Roasted fine ink, bitter herbs, soaked and stir-fried until charred, green stone, large dragon, stir-fried lacquer, five spirit resin, Beijing three-edge, mugwort, myrrh, tangerine peel, roasted oyster shell, each half an ounce. Fourteen large dates, roasted; one ounce of cleaned castor bean, wrapped in damp paper, burned until charred and stopped; white丁香, grinding antimony; wingless and legless蝱虫; one part each of spotted cat.

    Combine all into a fine powder, cook with vinegar to make dough balls the size of soap, form into muffins, and administer with the broth of the affected substance or warm flour soup. They must be chewed and swallowed; as the accumulation gradually shifts downward, take another ball when it moves further down. If normal circulation is needed, administer with flour soup. Blood clots, blockages, and persistent dysentery with pus and blood in both adults and children can all be treated here.[55p]

    Prescription for Treating Gu Li (Dysentery)

    Dry the leaves of the cypress and grind them into a powder, combine with equal parts of Sichuan Huanglian.

    Boil these two ingredients together to extract the juice, and administer it to treat children's severe abdominal pain, expelling black blood, tea-colored stool, or pus-like blood resembling sediment, known as gu li. This treatment is highly effective and can also eliminate the five organ toxins.

    Shenghui Pervinca Powder

    For treating persistent gu poison dysentery in children, characterized by heat and restlessness in the body.

    Ingredients: 2 taels of white pervinca root, 2 taels of ageratum, 1 fen of roasted drum skin (burnt), 0.5 taels of roasted licorice, 0.5 taels of dried blue leaf, and 0.3 taels of red peony and rhino horn shavings.

    Crush these herbs and sieve them to create a powder. For each dose, take 1 qian (approximately 3 grams), mix with a small cup of water and add 27 grains of fermented soybean, boil until reduced to one-fifth. Strain the mixture and give it warm, adjusting the dosage based on the child's size.

    Shenghui Huanglian Powder

    For treating children with gu poison blood dysentery and emaciation.

    Ingredients: 1 tael of Huanglian, lightly roasted; burnt drum skin (焦) until charred; half a tael each of white peony, roasted licorice, and blue-green herbs; and 0.3 taels of rhino horn shavings, white pervinca root, Huangqin, and chopped madder root.

    Crush these herbs and sieve them to make a powder. For each dose, take 1 qian, mix with a small cup of water, boil until it reduces to one-fifth, strain, and allow it to cool, adjusting dosage according to the child's size.[57p]

    Kong's Family Heirloom Recipe for Treating Poison.

    Capsella bursa-pastoris root.
    Pound it into a powder and take with a sip for immediate recovery. One method allows for mixing with ground earth and tree of heaven roots.

    Shuangjin Drink treats diarrhea, both red and white, occurring frequently day and night, as well as chronic diarrhea.

    • Large opium poppy husks, de-stemmed and ground finely, stir-fried with honey water until dry, one liang.
    • Large chuanxiong, ground finely, stir-fried with vinegar until dry, half a liang.

    Combine these two ingredients, further sun-dry or bake into a powder, and each time take one to two coins' worth, mixed with glutinous rice clear soup, or taken with warm honey water.

    Dragon Bone Soup (from "Thousand Golden Cures") treats slight fever in children, thirst leading to drink-induced diarrhea.

    • Dragon bone, roasted licorice, rhubarb, red stone resin, gypsum, cinnamon bark, cold water stone, and trichosanthes root, each two taels.
      Combine these eight ingredients, treat with wine and water, five cups each, boil twice, strain, and adjust dosage according to the child's size.

    Mai Men Dong Soup treats children in summer months, after taking strong medicine, with empty heat and thirst in the stomach.

    • Mai men dong, heart removed, roasted licorice, each four fen; stir-fried bitter orange, yellow root, ginseng, each three fen; dragon bone six fen.
      Chop these six ingredients, boil with two sheng of water until getting nine cups, strain, and divide for warm consumption.

    Dang Gui San treats children’s dysentery and thirst, with persistent abdominal pain. Lightly fry Dang Gui and Huang Lian to remove impurities; each three parts of Huang Qi, and five qian of processed Gan Jiang and lightly roasted Gan Cao turning slightly red.

    The above mixture should be crushed and sieved to a fine powder. Each dose is one qian, taken with one small cup of water, boiled down to one-fifth, strained, and can be given regardless of the time, adjusting the amount based on the child's size and temperature.

    Long Gu San treats children’s dysentery and thirst, with body heat and restlessness. One liang of Bai Long Gu, half a liang of Hu Huang Lian, and three parts each of Fu Shen, Ren Shen, Mao Gen, and roasted Mai Men Dong (heart removed).

    The above ingredients should be crushed and sieved to make a powder. Each dose is one qian, taken with one small cup of water, boiled down to one-fifth, strained, and taken warm.

    Lan Ye San treats children’s dysentery and thirst, with persistent heat and restlessness. Two fen of Lan Ye, one fen of red Fu Ling, one liang of calcined red Shi Zhi, lightly fried Huang Lian, winter melon seeds, and half a liang each of vinegar Pomegranate Peel (lightly fried).

    The above ingredients should be crushed and sieved to make a powder. Each dose is one qian, taken with one small cup of water, boiled down to one-fifth, strained, and then half a teaspoon of honey is added, boiled for an additional three to two boils, adjusting the amount based on the child's size and temperature.[62p]

    Dihu San: Treats children's diarrhea and thirst, or if there are five-colored harmful substances in the stool, leading to restless mind and spirit.
    Ingredients: Dihu (1 tael), White Poria (1 tael), and slightly roasted Huanglian (1 tael).
    Method: Grind the ingredients coarsely and sift to make a powder. Each dose is about 1 qian, boiled in a small cup of water until reduced to one-fifth, strain out the residue. The dosage should be adjusted according to the child's size, without strict timing.

    Huanglian San: Treats children's diarrhea, thirst, and heat, with an insatiable thirst.
    Ingredients: Slightly roasted Huanglian (0.5 tael), oyster powder (0.5 tael), slightly roasted Wumei (0.1 tael), licorice (0.1 tael), and Keli (0.1 tael) with the skin.
    Method: Grind the ingredients to make a powder. Each dose is 1 qian, boiled in a small cup of water until reduced to one-fifth, strain out the residue. The dosage should be adjusted according to the child's size, without strict timing.

    Ju Pi San: Treats children's persistent diarrhea and thirst.
    Ingredients: Ju pi (1 tael), Gualou root (0.3 tael), Poria (0.3 tael), and Ren Shen (0.5 tael).
    Method: Grind the ingredients finely to make a powder. No specific timing for taking. Mix with corn drink, take 0.5 qian, and adjust based on the child’s size.

    Gan Cao San: Treats children's persistent diarrhea and thirst.
    Ingredients: Roasted licorice (1 tael), slightly roasted Wumei (1 tael), and 2 Keli with skin.
    Method: Grind the ingredients to make a powder. Each dose is 1 qian, boiled in a small cup of water with a little fresh ginger until reduced to one-fifth, strain out the residue. Allow to cool, and adjust dosage according to the child's size, without strict timing.[63p]

    Huangqin Pill: Treats children's dysentery with incessant thirst, high fever, and abdominal pain.     Taishi Bureau Ginseng Powder: Harmonizes the central Qi, relieves nausea, and eliminates thirst.     Infant Qi Decoction: Treats children with high fever and dysentery, accompanied by thirst and aversion to cold.     2. Winter Melon Soup: Treats persistent thirst in children and diarrhea that does not cease.

    3. Zhang Huan's Stomach Strengthening Powder: Treats diarrhea, body heat, and thirst.

    4. Bi Xiang Dan: Treats children with post-vomiting and diarrhea, resulting in unquenchable thirst and inability to sleep, which can lead to wasting.

    Treasure Mirror Bamboo Dried Pill: Treats children's thirst and diarrhea.     Ginseng and White Cowpea Soup: Treats disharmony of the spleen and stomach, lack of appetite, vomiting and diarrhea, thirst and desire to drink water, as well as hyperactivity in children. Use one ounce each of ginseng and peeled, roasted white cowpeas, along with one ounce each of white atractylodes and poria, and half an ounce each of poppy seeds and honey-fried licorice, and yam. Grind these into powder. For each serving, use two qian (7.5 grams), with one cup of water, add two slices of ginger and half a jujube, then simmer until reduced by one-third, and drink orally. In case of abdominal pain, add perilla leaves to the decoction. If the child has hyperactivity, add peppermint during decoction.

    Zhang's Holy Cake is used to treat persistent diarrhea and abdominal pain in children, as well as rectal prolapse with bleeding. One tael of spirit yeast and one penny of greasy powder are to be mixed evenly. Then, blend the mixture with egg whites to achieve the right thickness. Form circular cakes about the size of a coin, and dry them over a fire until they turn yellow. Take one cake in the morning on an empty stomach together with an oil cake, followed by a small drink.

    Ji's Purple Frost Pills treat children with prolonged constipation, emaciation from rising chest illness, and severe abdominal pain from dysentery. Half a tael of Dingtou Daitie (substance) is roasted five times and soaked in vinegar five times. Combine one penny of frankincense, twenty-seven apricot kernels (frosted), one penny of cinnabar and broad wood fragrance, one-fifth of a penny of Xuan Huanglian (herb, with heads removed), half a penny of fine powder, a pinch of musk, two nutmeg seeds, and ten frost-hardened ba dou (seed).     Liu's formula from the External Platform can treat children with deficiency after diarrhea, hot palms and soles, and unresolved diarrhea. Three-thirds of tangerine peel and ginger are chopped and boiled in half a liter of cow's milk to reduce it to four portions. Strain and serve warm.[69p]

    Gathering Treasures Elephant Bean Pill

    For treating all types of dysentery and prolapse of the rectum:

    The vine seed, also known as elephant bean, grows in the mountainous forests of Guangnan and resembles purple-black ramie. Take this as a powder. For dysentery with blood, take two qian and mix with hot wine, and it must work within three doses. For white dysentery, take the kernels, crush and fry them slowly over low heat until they turn yellow-brown. Grind finely and sift it two times. If any white remains, fry it further until brown to make it into powder. Soak in steamed cake broth and mold into round balls the size of dried peas; bake slightly dry. Take fifteen to twenty pills with warm fragrant rice drink before meals, and the dysentery will stop immediately. For insect poison, five piles, and children's prolapse of the rectum, it can also be made into powder and taken with wine for immediate cure.[72p]

    For treating weakness of the large intestine and rectal prolapse:

    Baosheng Formula: For the treatment of long-term intestinal wind, hemorrhoids, and prolapse, where the intestines protrude, sometimes several inches, causing extreme pain. Children suffering from prolonged diarrhea often have this ailment. Use four taels of wubeizi, boil in five liters of water until bubbling, then add four taels of (shibu) saltpeter, and wash the affected area until the water cools, then stop. If there is a sensation of heat or pain, mix saliva with bear bile and apply it; the pain will then stop and gradually heal. In severe cases, wash three to five times to complete the treatment. Upon examining this medicine, (shibu) saltpeter can soften, and wubeizi can constrict; these two substances complement each other for this purpose. Alternatively, one can mix in powdered dry cockroach or spider and knead into warm cloth for even better effect. Adding dried spider is similar to the method in Ge's formula.

    Jiuyao Weisheng Formula: For the treatment of children’s rectal prolapse. Use equal parts of Xiangfuzi (Cyperus), and Jingjie (Schizonepeta) ground into a coarse powder. Each time, use three spoonfuls, boil it in a large bowl of water for several minutes and wash.

    Kushen Decoction: For the treatment of rectal prolapse and hemorrhoids. Use equal parts of Zhike (Bitter Orange), Huanglian (Coptis), Dahuang (Rhubarb), Gancao (Licorice), Jingjie, Kushen, Chishao (Red Peony), and Huangqin (Scutellaria). Grind into a powder, each time using five qian, boil with Cheqianzi (Plantago seeds) and straw for steaming wash.

    Moreover: for children with red or white diarrhea, take a handful of garlic, one liter of fermented soybeans, combine with three liters of water, boil until two liters remain, and divide into three doses.
    Moreover: mix one liter each of cypress leaves and sesame seed powder with five liters of water, boil until it bubbles three times; children under a hundred days should take three doses.
    Moreover: crush pomegranate juice and drink it.
    Moreover: burn beehive ash and mix with water to consume.
    Moreover: mix equal parts of burnt hair and deer antler ash; for a three-year-old, mix three qian with water and give three times a day.
    To treat children with red or white dysentery: use five qian each of white artemisia root juice and fresh rehmannia juice, simmer on low heat until it boils, and consume.
    Moreover: take one qian of fresh rehmannia juice.
    Moreover: on the fifth of May, take half a qian of toad ash mixed with water.
    To treat children with hot dysentery: boil papaya leaves and drink the infusion.

    To treat children with cold dysentery: crush smartweed leaves for juice, adjusting the amount based on the child's size. Another method uses mustard greens.
    Moreover: crush garlic and apply it to the feet.[77p]

    　　治小儿暴痢：小鲫鱼一头烧灰服之。　　又：烧鲤鱼骨服之。一方作龙骨。
    　　又:赤小豆末，酒和涂足下，日三度，油和亦得。
    　　治小儿蛊毒痢：蓝青汁一升二合，分为四服。
    　　治小儿渴痢：捣冬瓜汁饮之。

    　　小儿疟痢：用鸡膍胵黄皮烧存性，乳服。男用雌，女用雄。
    　　治小儿久痢脓湿(上匿下虫)：艾叶五升，以水一斗，煮取一升半，分为三服。
    　　小儿下痢，腹大且坚：用多垢故衣带切一升，水五升，煮一升，分三服。
    　　小儿泄痢噤口：大蒜捣贴两足心，亦可贴脐中。
    　　小儿下痢赤白：用麻油一合，捣和，蜜汤服之。 【《外台方》，下同】
    　　小儿疳痢困重者：用樗白皮捣粉，以水和枣作大馄饨子，日晒少时，又捣，如此三遍，以水煮熟，空肚吞七枚，重者不过七服。忌油腻热面毒物。　　又方：用樗根浓汁一蚬壳，和粟米泔等分灌下部，再度即瘥，其效如神。[78p]

    Treating children's acute dysentery: One small crucian carp, burned to ash and taken. Additionally: Burn the bones of a carp and take them. One recipe suggests using dragon bones.

    To treat children's toxic dysentery: One liter and two deciliters of blue-green juice, divided into four doses.

    To treat children's thirst and dysentery: Crush winter melon to extract juice and have them drink it.

    For children with malaria-related dysentery: Use the gall bladder from a chicken’s yellow skin, burned until fully cooked, and take with milk. Males should use the female gall bladder, females should use the male.

    To treat children's prolonged dysentery with pus and dampness (accompanied by worms): Five liters of mugwort leaves, boiled in ten liters of water to yield one and a half liters, divided into three doses.

    For children with diarrhea and a distended, hard abdomen: Take one liter of heavily soiled old clothing, five liters of water, boil to yield one liter, divided into three doses.

    For children with diarrhea and a locked mouth: Mash garlic and apply to the soles of the feet; it can also be applied to the navel.

    For children with mixed red and white diarrhea: Take one deciliter of sesame oil, mash and mix, and take with honey water.

    For children suffering from severe dysentery: Use white mulberry bark ground into powder, mix with water and jujube to make large dumplings, sun-dry briefly, then grind again. Repeat this three times, then boil in water until cooked. Consume seven of them on an empty stomach; those severely affected should not take more than seven doses. Avoid greasy, hot foods and toxic materials.

    Another recipe: Use a concentrated juice from the root of the mulberry tree with one clam shell, mix equally with corn wash and administer; recovery is swift, with miraculous effects.[78p]

    　　小儿洞痢：柏叶煮汁代茶饮之。 【《经验方》】
    　　小儿久痢：没石子二个，熬黄研末，作馄饨食之。 【《宫气方》】
    　　小儿下痢赤白，及水痢：云母粉半两，煮白粥调食之。 【《食医心鉴》】
    　　小儿白痢：用陈北艾四两、干姜炮三两为末，酢煮仓米糊丸桐子大，每服三十丸，空心米饮下。【《永类方》】
    　　小儿久痢，水谷不调：枳实捣末，饮服一二钱。 【《广利方》】
    　　小儿热痢：嫩黄瓜同蜜食，十余枚良。 【《海上名方》】
    　　小儿白痢似鱼冻者：白鸭杀取血，滚酒泡服，即止也。 【《摘元方》】
    　　小儿血痢：马齿苋菜杵汁三合煎沸，入蜜一合和服。 【《心镜》】
    　　小儿下痢赤白：用巴豆煨熟去油一钱，百草霜二钱研末，飞罗面煮糊丸黍米大，量儿用之。赤用甘草汤，白用米汤，赤白用姜汤下。【《全幼心鉴》】[79p]

    • For children with chronic dysentery: Boil two pieces of knotgrass in water and drink the infusion instead of tea.

    • For children with persistent dysentery: Take two pieces of dandelion root, roast until yellow, grind into powder, and prepare dumplings with it.

    • For children with red and white dysentery and watery dysentery: Use half a tael of muscovite powder and mix it with boiled plain congee to eat.

    • For children with white dysentery: Use four taels of aged mugwort and three taels of roasted ginger to make powder, cook it with millet porridge into pills the size of tung seeds, taking thirty pills each time, followed by rice water.

    • For children with persistent dysentery and unbalanced diet: Crush bitter orange into powder, and take one or two qian with water.

    • For children with heat dysentery: Eating tender cucumbers with honey, about ten or more, is beneficial.

    • For children with white dysentery resembling fish jelly: Kill a white duck and collect its blood, drink it mixed with hot wine for immediate effect.

    • For children with bloody dysentery: Use three heaping cups of purslane juice boiled, and add one cup of honey to mix and consume.

    • For children with dysentery characterized by red and white symptoms: Use one qian of prepared cowbane (after removing oil) and two qian of herbal frost, grind into powder, and cook into pills as big as millet, adjust dosage for the child. For red symptoms, use licorice soup; for white, use rice soup; and for mixed red and white, use ginger soup.[79p]

    　　小儿血痢：梁州榉皮二十分炙，犀角十二分，水三升，分三服取瘥。 【《古今经验方》】
    　　小儿秋痢：以粳米煮粥，熟时入干柿末，再煮三两沸食之，奶母亦食之。 【《食疗方》，下同】
    　　小儿下痢赤白：鸡肠草捣汁一合，和蜜服甚良。
    　　小儿刮肠噤口痢疾，闭目者至重：精猪肉一两，薄切炙香，以腻粉末半钱铺上令食，或置鼻头闻香，自然要食也。【《活幼口议》】
    　　小儿疳痢，羸瘦多睡，坐则闭目，食不下：用蚺蛇胆豆许二枚，煮通草汁研化，随意饮之，并涂五心下部。【《杨氏产乳》】
    　　治小儿赤痢：捣青蓝汁二升，分四服。 【《本事方》，下同】
    　　治小儿屎血：用甘草五分，以水六合，煎取二合，去滓，一岁儿一日服令尽。
    　　小儿蛊痢：生芐汁一升二合，分三四服，立效。 【《子母秘录》，下同】[80p]

    Children's blood dysentery: 20 grams of jujube bark from Liangzhou, 12 grams of rhinoceros horn, and 3 liters of water, divided into three doses for recovery.

    Children's autumn dysentery: Cook japonica rice into porridge, and when it's ready, add dried persimmon powder, then boil for another two to three minutes and eat it; nursing mothers should also consume this.

    Children's diarrhea with red and white stools: One cup of chicken intestine grass juice, mixed with honey, is very effective.

    For severe children's diarrhea with constipation and closed eyes: One ounce of finely sliced and roasted pork, sprinkled with half a penny's worth of greasy powder, should be eaten. Alternatively, place it near the nose for the aroma to stimulate appetite.

    Children's malnutrition and dysentery, being emaciated, sleeping a lot, eyes closed when sitting, and unable to eat: Use two beans of green snake bile, boil with the juice of dried herbs and strain it, for drinking as desired, and apply to the soles of the feet as well.

    To treat children's red dysentery: Crush indigo plant juice into two liters and divide into four doses.

    To treat children's stool with blood: Use five grams of licorice, mix with 6 liters of water, boil down to 2 cups, strain, and have a one-year-old child drink it all in one day.

    Children's poisonous dysentery: One and a half liters of fresh aspersum juice, divided into three or four doses, provides immediate effect.[80p]

    　　小儿下痢赤白作渴，得水又呕逆者：构叶炙香，以饮浆半升，浸至水绿，去叶，以木瓜一个切纳汁中，煮二三沸，细细饮之。
    　　小儿痢下赤白，体弱大困者：麻子仁三合，炒香研细末，每服一钱，浆水服立效。
    　　小儿下痢赤白多时，体弱不堪：以宣连用水浓煎和蜜，日服五六次。
    　　小儿下痢：用羚羊角中骨烧末，饮服方寸匕。
    　　小儿下痢：林檎、构子同杵汁，任意服之。
    　　小儿赤痢：捣青蓝汁二升，分四服。
    　　小儿无辜疳，下痢赤白：胡粉熟蒸熬令色变，以饮服半钱。
    　　小儿丹烦：柳叶一斤，水一斗，煮取汁三升，洗赤处，日七八度。
    　　小儿水痢，形乏不胜汤药：白脂石半两研粉，和白粥空肚食之。
    　　小儿夏秋间患痢：用京芍药、藿香叶、赤茯苓、陈皮各三分，泽泻、苏叶、葛粉各四分，甘草一分，生姜三片，同煎。【《穷乡便方》，下同】[81p]

    For children with diarrhea characterized by red and white stools and thirst, who vomit after drinking water: use the leaves of the prickly ash, roast them until fragrant, then brew half a liter of liquid until it turns green, strain out the leaves, add one chopped papaya, boil for two or three minutes, and have them drink it slowly.

    For children with prolonged red and white diarrhea, who are weak and significantly fatigued: use three parts of hemp seed, roast, grind into a fine powder, and give them one qian to take with rice water for immediate effect.

    For children with persistent red and white diarrhea, who are weak and unable to endure: use Xuanlian herb, boil in strong water and mix with honey, and have them take it five or six times a day.

    For children with diarrhea: burn and powder the bone of antelope horn, and give them a small spoonful to drink.

    For children with diarrhea: mash akebia and prickly ash together for juice, and let them take it as desired.

    For children with red diarrhea: crush indigo juice, two liters, divided into four doses.

    For children with malnutrition-related diarrhea presenting with red and white stools: steam and roast powdered gourd until it changes color, and have them take half a qian to drink.

    For children with irritability: use one jin of willow leaves, one dou of water, boil to extract three liters of juice, and wash the affected areas seven to eight times a day.

    For children with watery diarrhea who are weak and cannot bear the medicine: grind half liang of white lead stone into powder, mix with plain porridge, and have them eat it on an empty stomach.

    For children suffering from diarrhea in summer and autumn: use equal parts of white peony root, patchouli leaves, red poria, and aged tangerine peel (three portions each), and four portions each of ze xie (water plantain), perilla leaves, and kudzu powder, one portion of licorice, and three slices of fresh ginger, and boil them together.[81p]

    　　服前药后，如腹中痛，昼夜无度，下痢红白：用车前子、木通、枳壳、黄连各四分，条黄芩小者四分，白芍药生用、槟榔各三分，甘草一分，姜皮、灯心煎服；此不止，用香连丸。
    　　　　针灸

    　　《千金方》曰：小儿脱肛，灸顶上旋毛中三壮，即入。又灸尾翠骨三壮。又灸脐中随年壮。　　《圣惠方》曰：治秋深冷痢不止者，灸脐下二三寸动脉中三壮，炷如麦。　　《古今医统》曰：小儿脱肛，灸神关[神关　疑当作「神阙」。]三壮，禁针，神关一名气舍，当脐中。或针脊中五分，禁灸。脊中一名神宗，一名脊俞，在十一椎节下间。俛而取之。　　小儿脱肛，灸百会、龟尾。
    　　《证治准绳》曰：小儿脱肛者，灸脐中三壮。　　小儿脱肛久不瘥，及风癎中风，角弓反张，多哭，言语不择，发无时节，盛即吐沫者，取百会一六，灸七壮。在鼻直入发际五寸，顶中央旋毛中，可容炷如小麦大。[82p]

    When experiencing abdominal pain after taking medicine, without discernment day or night, and having a red and white diarrhea: use four parts each of Plantago seeds, Mu Tong, Zhi Ke, and Huang Lian, four parts of minor Huang Qin, three parts each of raw Bai Shao and Bing Lang, one part of Gan Cao, and decoct with ginger skin and lampwick; if this is not sufficient, use Xiang Lian pills.

    Acupuncture and Moxibustion

    "The Thousand Golden Prescriptions" states: for a child with prolapsed rectum, moxibustion should be applied to the top of the head in the center of the fontanelle three times, then to the tailbone three times, and to the navel three times according to the child's age. "The Holy Benefits Prescriptions" says: to treat unrelenting deep cold diarrhea in autumn, moxibustion should be applied to the artery about two or three inches below the navel three times, using moxa the size of millet. "The Ancient and Modern Medical Compilation" states: for a child with prolapsed rectum, moxibustion should be applied to Shen Guan (which is likely to be Shen Que) three times, and needles should be avoided. Shen Guan, also called Qi She, is located at the center of the navel. Alternatively, acupuncture can be performed on the spine at five fen, but moxibustion should be avoided. The spine, called Shen Zong or Ji Yu, is located between the eleventh vertebrae. Leaning forward obtain it. For children with prolapsed rectum, moxibustion should also be applied to Bai Hui and Gui Wei.

    "The Principles for Diagnosis and Treatment" states: for a child with prolapsed rectum, moxibustion should be applied to the center of the navel three times. If the prolapse has persisted and is accompanied by wind-cerebral issues, arching back, excessive crying, incoherent speech, and paroxysmal drooling, apply moxibustion at Bai Hui for six times. Moxibustion should penetrate five inches directly at the hairline and in the center of the top of the head, capable of holding moxa the size of a small wheat grain.[82p]

    　　　　医案

    　　《儒门事亲》曰：一宦家小儿病痢，自郾头车，载之朱葛寺，入门而死。戴人曰：有病远行，不可车载马驼。病已扰矣，又以车动摇之，是为重扰，宜即死。
    　　万氏《幼科发挥》曰：一儿五岁病痢，医用药治之，痢转甚，其脾胃中气下陷也。予用参苓白朮散调之，十日痢止。予辞归。有惑者谓其父曰：无积不成痢。富家之子，多是肉积。吾有阿魏尝用治痢有效。父惑而听之，乃以阿魏作丸如小豆大，连服三丸，其子昏睡。予至，以服阿魏丸告予。予惊曰：阿魏虽去肉积，大损元气，令郎脾胃已弱，岂可服之？父曰：病安而喜睡，未醒也。予谓乳母叫之，则目露睛，气已绝矣。
    　　一小儿下痢赤白，里急后重，腹时痛，用黄连丸而痊。后伤食，复变痢，欲呕少食，用五味异功散加木香三分、黄连二分、吴茱萸一分，数剂而愈。
    　　一小儿患痢，口干发热，用白朮散煎与恣饮，时以白朮散送香连丸而安。[83p]

    Medical Case Records

    The "Confucian Teachings on Filial Piety" states: A child from an official's family suffered from dysentery. He was taken by carriage from Yantou to Zhuge Temple and died upon entering. A person said: When ill, one should not be transported by carriage or on horseback. The illness was already severe, and moving him in a vehicle caused further disturbance, which is fatal.

    The "Pediatrics" by the Wan family states: A five-year-old child had dysentery. The physician treated him with medicine, but the dysentery worsened, causing the energy in his spleen and stomach to sink. I used a formula of ginseng, poria, and white atracylodes to adjust his condition, and after ten days, the dysentery ceased. I took my leave. Some skeptics said to the father: "No accumulation leads to dysentery. For children from wealthy families, it's mostly due to meat accumulation. I have found ferula (asafetida) effective for treating dysentery.” The father, confused, listened to them and made pills of ferula the size of small beans, giving his son three of them, after which the child fell into a deep sleep. When I arrived and was informed he had taken the ferula pills, I was shocked and said: "While ferula may dispel meat accumulation, it greatly harms vital energy. Your son’s spleen and stomach are already weak; how can he take it?" The father replied: "He is at peace and sleeps heavily; he has not awakened." I suggested to the wet nurse to call him, and as he opened his eyes, his breath had already ceased.

    A young child had dysentery with red and white discharge, feeling urgency and heaviness afterward, experiencing abdominal pain at times. He was treated with Huanglian pills and recovered. Later, he had food injuries, causing a recurrence of dysentery, with a desire to vomit and a poor appetite. I prescribed a modified Wuwei Yigong powder, adding three parts of wood fragrant, two parts of Huanglian, and one part of Wuzhuyu, and after several doses, he recovered.

    A small child suffered from dysentery, presenting with dry mouth and fever. I administered Baizhu powder and allowed him to drink freely, while at times using Baizhu powder to facilitate taking Xianglian pills, and he became stable.[83p]

    　　一小儿久痢，里急后重，欲去不去，手足并冷，此胃气虚寒下陷也，用补中益气汤加木香、补骨脂，倍加升麻、柴胡而愈。
    　　一小儿久痢，作渴发热，饮汤，用白朮散为主，佐以人参二两、黄连一两，炒黑为丸，时服数粒，尽剂而痊。
    　　一小儿作泻不乳，服克伐之剂，变痢，腹痛后重，余用补中益气汤送香连丸，又用香砂助胃膏、六君子汤而愈。
    　　一小儿伤乳食，不时呕吐，杂用消导之药，变痢不止，先用六君、木香渐愈，后用七味白朮散而痊。
    　　一小儿伤乳食，吐泻变赤痢，后重腹痛，先用香连丸而愈。又乳食过多腹痛，先用保和丸一服痛止，又用五味异功散加木香二剂而愈。
    　　一小儿下痢，腹痛阴冷，小便短少，用五味异功散加肉豆蔻顿愈。复作呕吐咽酸，或用巴豆之药，连泻五次，饮食顿减，手足并冷。余用五味异功散加木香、干姜，饮食少进；倍用干姜，又四剂，手足温和而痢亦痊。[84p]

    A young child had a long-lasting case of diarrhea, experiencing urgency and heaviness in the lower abdomen, wanting to relieve themselves but unable to, with cold hands and feet. This was due to a deficiency of stomach energy and cold sinking down. The prescription used was a modified Baizhong Yiqi Decoction with the addition of Mu Xiang and Bu Guo Zhi, and an increased amount of Sheng Ma and Chai Hu, leading to recovery.

    Another child suffered from prolonged diarrhea, thirst, and fever. They drank soup, and a formula based on Baizhu San was used, combined with two taels of Ren Shen and one tael of Huang Lian, fried and made into pills. Taking several pills over time led to recovery.

    A child experienced diarrhea without breastfeeding, took a purging remedy, which then turned into diarrhea with abdominal pain and heaviness afterward. The remaining treatment involved sending Xiang Lian Wan with Baizhong Yiqi Decoction and using Xiang Sha to assist the stomach with Liujunzi Decoction until recovery.

    A child injured from milk and food frequently vomited. Various digestive aids were used, but the diarrhea did not stop. Initially, Liujunzi and Mu Xiang led to gradual improvement, followed by the use of Qiwwei Baizhu San, resulting in recovery.

    Another child who injured their digestion from milk and food suffered from vomiting, diarrhea, and turning to dysentery, accompanied by abdominal pain and heaviness. They initially took Xiang Lian Wan and recovered. If they consumed too much milk and food leading to abdominal pain, they first used Baohe Wan to stop the pain, then took five flavors Yigong San with added Mu Xiang in two doses, resulting in recovery.

    A child with diarrhea experienced abdominal pain and coldness, with scanty urination. They were treated with five flavors Yigong San plus Rou Dou Kou, leading to immediate recovery. If vomiting and sour regurgitation occurred, using Ba Dou led to five bouts of diarrhea, decreasing appetite and experiencing cold hands and feet. The remaining treatment involved five flavors Yigong San combined with Mu Xiang and Gan Jiang, with little food intake; after doubling the dosage of Gan Jiang and taking four more doses, their hands and feet became warm, and the diarrhea also healed.[84p]

    　　一小儿痢后，腹胀作呕，大便不实，小便不利，诸药不应。余先用五味异功散加木香、肉果数服，二便少调；又数剂诸证少愈；用八味丸补命门之火，腹胀渐消；用金匮加减肾气丸，诸证顿退；又用四君子、升麻、柴胡而全安。
    　　一小儿患痢，喘嗽不已，此肺气虚也，用六君子加木香为末，每服钱许，以人参陈米姜汤调服，即睡，乳食少进；又二服而喘嗽顿安，乃用四君子汤而痊。
    　　一小儿痢后发热烦躁，用四君、当归、升麻、柴胡顿安，又用补中益气汤而愈。又伤食作泻，前证复作，吞酸，先用异功散加吴茱萸、木香为末，二服吞酸悉止，乃去茱萸、木香治之而安。
    　　一小儿痢后烦躁作渴，面赤，脉大按之如无，此血脱烦躁也，先用当归补血汤，又用五味异功散加升麻、当归而安。又伤食作泻不已，复烦躁，用异功散为主，佐以八珍汤而安。
    [85p]

    A child developed diarrhea, resulting in abdominal distension, vomiting, loose stools, and difficulty urinating, with little response to various medicines. I first administered a modified Wuwei Yigong San with added Muxiang and Rouguo, leading to slight improvement in urination and defecation; after several doses, symptoms mildly improved. I then used the Bawei Wan to nourish the fire at the life gate, gradually reducing abdominal distension. The Jinkui Jiadianshen Wan was then given, and symptoms quickly subsided; I also used the Sijunzi and herbs like Shengma and Chaihu for overall stability.

    For another child suffering from diarrhea, persistent coughing and wheezing indicated a deficiency of lung qi. I used a modified Liujunzi San to powder with Muxiang, administering a small amount mixed with ginseng, aged rice, and ginger soup, followed by sleep and minimal food intake. After two doses, coughing and wheezing significantly improved, so I switched to Sijunzi Tang, leading to recovery.

    A different child post-diarrhea exhibited fever and irritability, treated effectively with Sijunzi Tang, Danggui, Shengma, and Chaihu, leading to immediate relief; I then used Buzhong Yiqi Tang for their recovery. Due to subsequent food injury causing diarrhea and recurring symptoms, including acid regurgitation, I initially employed Yigong San with added Wuzhuyu and Muxiang in powdered form. After two doses, the acid reflux ceased, and then I removed Wuzhuyu and Muxiang for resolution.

    Another child post-diarrhea exhibited irritability, thirst, flushed face, and a weak pulse suggestive of blood deficiency. I first prescribed Danggui Buxue Tang, followed by a modified Wuwei Yigong San with Shengma and Danggui for stabilization. In cases of ongoing food injury causing diarrhea and persistent irritability, the primary treatment continued with Yigong San, complemented by Bazhen Tang for stability.[85p]
